\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ very\ simply\ rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ the\ bit\ from\ not\ used\ last\ word\ from\ temp\_table\ is\ set\ to\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ we're\ rouding\ the\ lowest\ word\ in\ the\ table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00285\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ in\ fact\ there\ should\ be\ a\ normal\ addition\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00286\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ we\ don't\ use\ Add()\ or\ AddTwoInts()\ because\ these\ methods\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00287\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ can\ set\ a\ carry\ and\ then\ there'll\ be\ a\ small\ problem}}
